A. Carucci\n\n\n// Purpose: Load YAML configs and JSON schemas from 09_Reference/Standards\n\n\nimport os\nimport json\nimport re\nfrom pathlib import Path\nfrom typing import Any, Dict, Optional\n\n\nimport yaml\n\n\nclass ConfigLoader:\n    \"\"\"Load and validate configuration files.\"\"\"\n\n\ndef __init__(self, config_dir: Path = None):\n    self.config_dir = config_dir or Path(__file__).parents[2] / \"config\"\n    self._schemas_config: Optional[Dict] = None\n\ndef load_yaml(self, filename: str) -> Dict[str, Any]:\n    \"\"\"Load YAML config with variable expansion.\"\"\"\n    filepath = self.config_dir / filename\n    if not filepath.exists():\n        raise FileNotFoundError(f\"Config not found: {filepath}\")\n    \n    with open(filepath, \"r\", encoding=\"utf-8\") as f:\n        raw = yaml.safe_load(f)\n    \n    return self._expand_variables(raw, raw)\n\ndef _expand_variables(self, obj: Any, context: Dict) -> Any:\n    \"\"\"Recursively expand ${var} references.\"\"\"\n    if isinstance(obj, str):\n        pattern = r\"\\$\\{(\\w+)\\}\"\n        matches = re.findall(pattern, obj)\n        for var in matches:\n            if var in context:\n                obj = obj.replace(f\"${{{var}}}\", str(context[var]))\n        return obj\n    elif isinstance(obj, dict):\n        return {k: self._expand_variables(v, context) for k, v in obj.items()}\n    elif isinstance(obj, list):\n        return [self._expand_variables(item, context) for item in obj]\n    return obj\n\ndef load_schema(self, schema_key: str) -> Dict[str, Any]:\n    \"\"\"Load JSON schema from 09_Reference/Standards.\"\"\"\n    if self._schemas_config is None:\n        self._schemas_config = self.load_yaml(\"schemas.yaml\")\n    \n    schema_path = self._schemas_config.get(\"schemas\", {}).get(schema_key)\n    if not schema_path:\n        raise KeyError(f\"Schema key not found: {schema_key}\")\n    \n    path = Path(schema_path)\n    if not path.exists():\n        raise FileNotFoundError(f\"Schema file not found: {path}\")\n    \n    with open(path, \"r\", encoding=\"utf-8\") as f:\n        return json.load(f)\n\ndef validate_all_paths(self) -> Dict[str, bool]:\n    \"\"\"Verify all referenced schema/mapping files exist.\"\"\"\n    if self._schemas_config is None:\n        self._schemas_config = self.load_yaml(\"schemas.yaml\")\n    \n    results = {}\n    for section in [\"schemas\", \"mappings\", \"config\"]:\n        for key, path in self._schemas_config.get(section, {}).items():\n            # Handle glob patterns\n            if \"*\" in str(path):\n                results[f\"{section}. {key}\"] = len(list(Path(path).parent.glob(Path(path).name))) > 0\n            else:\n                results[f\"{section}. {key}\"] = Path(path).exists()\n    return results\n\n\nConvenience functions\n\n\n_loader: Optional[ConfigLoader] = None\n\n\ndef get_loader() -> ConfigLoader:\n    global _loader\n    if _loader is None:\n        _loader = ConfigLoader()\n    return _loader\n\n\ndef load_config(name: str) -> Dict[str, Any]:\n    return get_loader().load_yaml(name)\n\n\ndef load_schema(key: str) -> Dict[str, Any]:\n    return get_loader().load_schema(key)\n\n\ndef validate_paths() -> Dict[str, bool]:\n    return get_loader().validate_all_paths()\n\n\n\nImmediate Action Items\n\n\nCreate the 3 config YAML files — copy templates from NEXT_STEPS.md, adjust paths\n\nCreate shared/config/loader.py — use skeleton above\n\nCreate package files — requirements.txt, A. Carucci\n\n\n// Purpose: Load YAML configs and JSON schemas from 09_Reference/Standards with variable expansion\n\n\nimport json\nimport logging\nimport re\nfrom glob import glob\nfrom pathlib import Path\nfrom typing import Any, Dict, List, Optional, Union\n\n\nimport yaml\n\n\nlogger = logging.getLogger(name)\n\n\nclass ConfigLoader:\n    \"\"\"\n    Load and validate configuration files with variable expansion.\n\n\nSupports:\n- YAML configuration files with ${variable} expansion\n- JSON schema loading from 09_Reference/Standards\n- Glob pattern matching for wildcard paths\n- Path validation for all referenced files\n\"\"\"\n\ndef __init__(self, config_dir: Optional[Path] = None):\n    \"\"\"\n    Initialize ConfigLoader.\n    \n    Args:\n        config_dir: Path to config directory.

Defaults to project's config/ folder.\n    \"\"\"\n    if config_dir is None:\n        # Navigate from shared/utils/ up to project root, then to config/\n        self.config_dir = Path(__file__).parents[2] / \"config\"\n    else:\n        self.config_dir = Path(config_dir)\n    \n    self._cache: Dict[str, Dict] = {}\n    self._schemas_config: Optional[Dict] = None\n    \n    logger.debug(f\"ConfigLoader initialized with config_dir: {self.config_dir}\")\n\ndef load_yaml(self, filename: str, use_cache: bool = True) -> Dict[str, Any]:\n    \"\"\"\n    Load YAML config file with variable expansion.\n    \n    Args:\n        filename: Name of YAML file (e.g., 'schemas.yaml')\n        use_cache: Whether to use cached result if available\n        \n    Returns:\n        Parsed and expanded configuration dictionary\n        \n    Raises:\n        FileNotFoundError: If config file doesn't exist\n        yaml.YAMLError: If YAML parsing fails\n    \"\"\"\n    cache_key = f\"yaml:{filename}\"\n    if use_cache and cache_key in self._cache:\n        logger.debug(f\"Returning cached config: {filename}\")\n        return self._cache[cache_key]\n    \n    filepath = self.config_dir / filename\n    if not filepath.exists():\n        raise FileNotFoundError(f\"Configuration file not found: {filepath}\")\n    \n    logger.info(f\"Loading config: {filepath}\")\n    \n    with open(filepath, \"r\", encoding=\"utf-8\") as f:\n        raw_config = yaml.safe_load(f)\n    \n    if raw_config is None:\n        raw_config = {}\n    \n    # Build context from top-level string values for variable expansion\n    context = {k: v for k, v in raw_config.items() if isinstance(v, str)}\n    expanded = self._expand_variables(raw_config, context)\n    \n    if use_cache:\n        self._cache[cache_key] = expanded\n    \n    return expanded\n\ndef _expand_variables(self, obj: Any, context: Dict[str, str]) -> Any:\n    \"\"\"\n    Recursively expand ${variable} references in configuration.\n    \n    Args:\n        obj: Object to expand (str, dict, list, or other)\n        context: Dictionary of variable names to values\n        \n    Returns:\n        Object with all ${var} references expanded\n    \"\"\"\n    if isinstance(obj, str):\n        # Find all ${variable} patterns\n        pattern = r\"\\$\\{(\\w+)\\}\"\n        \n        def replacer(match):\n            var_name = match.group(1)\n            if var_name in context:\n                return str(context[var_name])\n            logger.warning(f\"Undefined variable in config: ${{{var_name}}}\")\n            return match.group(0)  # Return original if not found\n        \n        return re.sub(pattern, replacer, obj)\n    \n    elif isinstance(obj, dict):\n        return {k: self._expand_variables(v, context) for k, v in obj.items()}\n    \n    elif isinstance(obj, list):\n        return [self._expand_variables(item, context) for item in obj]\n    \n    return obj\n\ndef load_schema(self, schema_key: str) -> Dict[str, Any]:\n    \"\"\"\n    Load JSON schema from 09_Reference/Standards.\n    \n    Args:\n        schema_key: Key from schemas.yaml (e.g., 'canonical', 'cad', 'rms')\n        \n    Returns:\n        Parsed JSON schema dictionary\n        \n    Raises:\n        KeyError: If schema_key not found in schemas.yaml\n        FileNotFoundError: If schema file doesn't exist\n        json.JSONDecodeError: If JSON parsing fails\n    \"\"\"\n    if self._schemas_config is None:\n        self._schemas_config = self.load_yaml(\"schemas.yaml\")\n    \n    schemas = self._schemas_config.get(\"schemas\", {})\n    if schema_key not in schemas:\n        available = list(schemas.keys())\n        raise KeyError(\n            f\"Schema key '{schema_key}' not found. Available: {available}\"\n        )\n    \n    schema_path = Path(schemas[schema_key])\n    \n    if not schema_path.exists():\n        raise FileNotFoundError(f\"Schema file not found: {schema_path}\")\n    \n    logger.info(f\"Loading schema '{schema_key}': {schema_path}\")\n    \n    with open(schema_path, \"r\", encoding=\"utf-8\") as f:\n        return json.load(f)\n\ndef load_mapping(self, mapping_key: str) -> Union[Dict[str, Any], List[Path]]:\n    \"\"\"\n    Load mapping file(s) from 09_Reference/Standards.\n    \n    Supports glob patterns (e.g., 'call_types_*.csv').\n    \n    Args:\n        mapping_key: Key from schemas.yaml mappings section\n        \n    Returns:\n        For JSON: Parsed dictionary\n        For glob patterns: List of matching file paths\n        For other files: File path\n        \n    Raises:\n        KeyError: If mapping_key not found\n        FileNotFoundError: If file(s) not found\n    \"\"\"\n    if self._schemas_config is None:\n        self._schemas_config = self.load_yaml(\"schemas.yaml\")\n    \n    mappings = self._schemas_config.get(\"mappings\", {})\n    if mapping_key not in mappings:\n        available = list(mappings.keys())\n        raise KeyError(\n            f\"Mapping key '{mapping_key}' not found. Available: {available}\"\n        )\n    \n    mapping_path = mappings[mapping_key]\n    \n    # Handle glob patterns\n    if \"*\" in mapping_path:\n        matched_files = sorted(glob(mapping_path))\n        if not matched_files:\n            raise FileNotFoundError(\n                f\"No files matched pattern: {mapping_path}\"\n            )\n        logger.info(f\"Glob pattern matched {len(matched_files)} files\")\n        return [Path(f) for f in matched_files]\n    \n    path = Path(mapping_path)\n    \n    if not path.exists():\n        raise FileNotFoundError(f\"Mapping file not found: {path}\")\n    \n    # Load JSON mappings directly\n    if path.suffix == \".json\":\n        logger.info(f\"Loading mapping '{mapping_key}': {path}\")\n        with open(path, \"r\", encoding=\"utf-8\") as f:\n            return json.load(f)\n    \n    # Return path for non-JSON files (markdown, csv, etc. )\n    return path\n\ndef load_config_file(self, config_key: str) -> Union[Dict[str, Any], Path]:\n    \"\"\"\n    Load runtime configuration file from config section.\n    \n    Args:\n        config_key: Key from schemas.yaml config section\n        \n    Returns:\n        For JSON: Parsed dictionary\n        For other files: File path\n    \"\"\"\n    if self._schemas_config is None:\n        self._schemas_config = self.load_yaml(\"schemas.yaml\")\n    \n    configs = self._schemas_config.get(\"config\", {})\n    if config_key not in configs:\n        available = list(configs.keys())\n        raise KeyError(\n            f\"Config key '{config_key}' not found. Available: {available}\"\n        )\n    \n    config_path = Path(configs[config_key])\n    \n    if not config_path.exists():\n        raise FileNotFoundError(f\"Config file not found: {config_path}\")\n    \n    if config_path.suffix == \".json\":\n        logger.info(f\"Loading config '{config_key}': {config_path}\")\n        with open(config_path, \"r\", encoding=\"utf-8\") as f:\n            return json.load(f)\n    \n    return config_path\n\ndef validate_all_paths(self) -> Dict[str, bool]:\n    \"\"\"\n    Verify all referenced schema, mapping, and config files exist.\n    \n    Returns:\n        Dictionary mapping path identifiers to existence status (True/False)\n    \"\"\"\n    if self._schemas_config is None:\n        self._schemas_config = self.load_yaml(\"schemas.yaml\")\n    \n    results = {}\n    \n    for section in [\"schemas\", \"mappings\", \"config\"]:\n        section_data = self._schemas_config.get(section, {})\n        \n        for key, path_str in section_data.items():\n            full_key = f\"{section}. {key}\"\n            \n            # Handle glob patterns\n            if \"*\" in str(path_str):\n                matched = glob(path_str)\n                results[full_key] = len(matched) > 0\n                if matched:\n                    logger.debug(f\"✓ {full_key}: {len(matched)} files matched\")\n                else:\n                    logger.warning(f\"✗ {full_key}: No files matched pattern\")\n            else:\n                exists = Path(path_str).exists()\n                results[full_key] = exists\n                if exists:\n                    logger.debug(f\"✓ {full_key}: Found\")\n                else:\n                    logger.warning(f\"✗ {full_key}: NOT FOUND - {path_str}\")\n    \n    return results\n\ndef get_validation_summary(self) -> str:\n    \"\"\"\n    Generate human-readable validation summary.\n    \n    Returns:\n        Formatted string with path validation results\n    \"\"\"\n    results = self.validate_all_paths()\n    \n    lines = [\"Schema/Mapping Path Validation Summary\", \"=\" * 45]\n    \n    found = sum(1 for v in results.values() if v)\n    total = len(results)\n    \n    lines.append(f\"Found: {found}/{total} paths\\n\")\n    \n    for key, exists in sorted(results.items()):\n        status = \"✓\" if exists else \"✗ MISSING\"\n        lines.append(f\"  {status} {key}\")\n    \n    return \"\\n\".join(lines)\n\ndef clear_cache(self):\n    \"\"\"Clear all cached configurations.\"\"\"\n    self._cache.clear()\n    self._schemas_config = None\n    logger.debug(\"Configuration cache cleared\")\n\n\nModule-level singleton and convenience functions\n\n\n_loader: Optional[ConfigLoader] = None\n\n\ndef get_loader(config_dir: Optional[Path] = None) -> ConfigLoader:\n    \"\"\"\n    Get or create the singleton ConfigLoader instance.\n\n\nArgs:\n    config_dir: Optional custom config directory\n    \nReturns:\n    ConfigLoader instance\n\"\"\"\nglobal _loader\nif _loader is None or config_dir is not None:\n    _loader = ConfigLoader(config_dir)\nreturn _loader\n\n\ndef load_config(name: str) -> Dict[str, Any]:\n    \"\"\"\n    Convenience function to load a YAML config file.\n\n\nArgs:\n    name: Config filename (e.g., 'validation_rules.yaml')\n    \nReturns:\n    Parsed configuration dictionary\n\"\"\"\nreturn get_loader().load_yaml(name)\n\n\ndef load_schema(key: str) -> Dict[str, Any]:\n    \"\"\"\n    Convenience function to load a JSON schema.\n\n\nArgs:\n    key: Schema key from schemas.yaml (e.g., 'cad', 'rms', 'canonical')\n    \nReturns:\n    Parsed JSON schema dictionary\n\"\"\"\nreturn get_loader().load_schema(key)\n\n\ndef validate_paths() -> Dict[str, bool]:\n    \"\"\"\n    Convenience function to validate all configured paths.\n\n\nReturns:\n    Dictionary mapping path identifiers to existence status\n\"\"\"\nreturn get_loader().validate_all_paths()\n\n\ndef print_validation_summary():\n    \"\"\"Print formatted validation summary to stdout.\"\"\"\n    print(get_loader().get_validation_summary())\n\n\nCLI support for standalone validation\n\n\nif name == \"main\":\n    logging.basicConfig(\n        level=logging.INFO,\n        format=\"%(asctime)s - %(levelname)s - %(message)s\"\n    )\n    print_validation_summary()\n\n\n\n3a. \"\"\"\n    Stub: Calculate 0-100 quality score.\n\n\nTODO: Replace with import from shared.validators.quality_scorer\n\"\"\"\nlogger.debug(\"Quality scoring stub called\")\n# Simple placeholder: 100 if no errors, otherwise proportional\nif validation_results[\"total_records\"] == 0:\n    return 0.0\nvalid_ratio = validation_results[\"valid_records\"] / validation_results[\"total_records\"]\nreturn round(valid_ratio * 100, 2)\n\n\n=============================================================================\n\n\nCore Functions\n\n\n=============================================================================\n\n\ndef load_source_file(source: Dict) -> Optional[pd.DataFrame]:\n    \"\"\"\n    Load a single CAD source file.\n\n\nArgs:\n    source: Source configuration dict with path, year, expected_records\n    \nReturns:\n    DataFrame or None if file not found\n\"\"\"\nfilepath = Path(source[\"path\"])\nyear = source[\"year\"]\nexpected = source.get(\"expected_records\", 0)\nsheet = source.get(\"sheet_name\")\n\nif not filepath.exists():\n    logger.error(f\"[{year}] File not found: {filepath}\")\n    return None\n\nlogger.info(f\"[{year}] Loading: {filepath.name}\")\n\ntry:\n    # Load Excel file\n    df = pd.read_excel(\n        filepath,\n        sheet_name=sheet if else 0\n    \n    logger.info(f\"[{year}] Loaded {actual:,} records (expected ~{expected:,}, variance: {variance:.1f}%)\")\n    \n    # Add source tracking\n    df[\"_source_year\"] = year\n    df[\"_source_file\"] = filepath.name\n    \n    return df\n    \nexcept Exception as e:\n    logger.error(f\"[{year}] Failed to load: {e}\")\n    return None\n\n\ndef compute_file_hash(filepath: Path) -> str:\n    \"\"\"Compute MD5 hash of file for audit trail.\"\"\"\n    hasher = hashlib.md5()\n    with open(filepath, \"rb\") as f:\n        for chunk in iter(lambda: f.read(8192), b\"\"):\n            hasher.update(chunk)\n    return hasher.hexdigest()\n\n\ndef detect_gaps(df: pd.DataFrame, date_column: str = \"DateOfCall\") -> pd.DataFrame:\n    \"\"\"\n    Detect missing dates or low-count days in the dataset.\n\n\nArgs:\n    df: Consolidated DataFrame\n    date_column: Name of date column\n    \nReturns:\n    DataFrame with gap analysis\n\"\"\"\nif date_column not in df.columns:\n    logger.warning(f\"Date column '{date_column}' not found for gap detection\")\n    return pd.DataFrame()\n\ntry:\n    # Convert to datetime\n    dates = pd.to_datetime(df[date_column], errors=\"coerce\")\n    \n    # Count records per day\n    daily_counts = dates.dt.date.value_counts().sort_index()\n    \n    # Find date range\n    min_date = daily_counts.index.min()\n    max_date = daily_counts.index.max()\n    \n    # Generate complete date range\n    full_range = pd.date_range(start=min_date, end=max_date, freq=\"D\")\n    \n    # Find missing dates\n    missing = set(full_range.date) - set(daily_counts.index)\n    \n    # Find low-count days (threshold from config)\n    low_threshold = 50\n    low_days = daily_counts[daily_counts < low_threshold]\n    \n    gaps = []\n    for date in sorted(missing):\n        gaps.append({\"date\": date, \"issue\": \"missing\", \"count\": 0})\n    for date, count in low_days.items():\n        gaps.append({\"date\": date, \"issue\": \"low_count\", \"count\": count})\n    \n    gap_df = pd.DataFrame(gaps)\n    \n    if len(gap_df) > 0:\n        logger.warning(f\"Gap detection found {len(gap_df)} issues\")\n    else:\n        logger.info(\"No gaps detected in date coverage\")\n    \n    return gap_df\n    \nexcept Exception as e:\n    logger.error(f\"Gap detection failed: {e}\")\n    return pd.DataFrame()\n\n\ndef deduplicate_records(df: pd.DataFrame, key_column: str = \"ReportNumberNew\") -> pd.DataFrame:\n    \"\"\"\n    Remove duplicate records based on key column.\n\n\nArgs:\n    df: DataFrame to deduplicate\n    key_column: Column to use as unique identifier\n    \nReturns:\n    Deduplicated DataFrame\n\"\"\"\nif key_column not in df.columns:\n    logger.warning(f\"Dedup key '{key_column}' not found, skipping deduplication\")\n    return df\n\nbefore = len(df)\n\n# Keep first occurrence (earliest year due to loading order)\ndf_deduped = df.drop_duplicates(subset=[key_column], keep=\"first\")\n\nafter = len(df_deduped)\nremoved = before - after\n\nif removed > 0:\n    dup_rate = removed / before * 100\n    logger.info(f\"Deduplication: removed {removed:,} duplicates ({dup_rate:.2f}%)\")\nelse:\n    logger.info(\"No duplicates found\")\n\nreturn df_deduped\n\n\ndef generate_consolidation_report(\n    metrics: Dict[str, Any],\n    output_dir: Path,\n) -> None:\n    \"\"\"\n    Generate consolidation report files.\n\n\nArgs:\n    metrics: Dictionary of consolidation metrics\n    output_dir: Directory for report files\n\"\"\"\nimport json\n\noutput_dir.mkdir(parents=True, exist_ok=True)\n\n# JSON metrics\njson_path = output_dir / \"consolidation_metrics.json\"\nwith open(json_path, \"w\", encoding=\"utf-8\") as f:\n findings\n\n\ndef consolidate(\n    dry_run: bool = False,\n    validate_only: bool = False,\n) -> Optional[pd.DataFrame]:\n    \"\"\"\n    Main consolidation workflow.\n\n\nArgs:\n    dry_run: If True, only validate inputs without processing\n    validate_only: If True, validate but don't save outputs\n    \nReturns:\n    Consolidated DataFrame or None on failure\n\"\"\"\nstart_time = -------------------------------------------------------------------------\nlogger.info(\"\\n[Step 1/7] Validating configuration...\")\n\npath_results = validate_paths()\nmissing = [k for k, v in path_results.items() if not v]\nif missing:\n    logger.warning(f\"Missing schema paths: {missing}\")\n    logger.warning(\"Continuing with available schemas...\")\n\n# Load configurations\ntry:\n    sources_config = load_config(\"consolidation_sources.yaml\")\n    validation_config = load_config(\"validation_rules.yaml\")\nexcept FileNotFoundError as e:\n    logger.error(f\"Configuration not found: {e}\")\n    return None\n\nsources = sources_config.get(\"sources\", [])\nlogger.info(f\"Found {len(sources)} source files to process\")\n\nif dry_run:\n    logger.info(\"\\n[DRY RUN] Validating source files exist...\")\n    for src in sources:\n        path = Path(src[\"path\"])\n        status = \"✓\" if path.exists() else \"✗ MISSING\"\n        logger.info(f\"  {status} [{src['year']}] {path.name}\")\n    logger.info(\"\\n[DRY RUN] Complete. No files processed.\")\n    return None\n\n# -------------------------------------------------------------------------\n# Step 2: Load schema\n# -------------------------------------------------------------------------\nlogger.info(\"\\n[Step 2/7] Loading CAD schema...\")\n\ntry:\n    cad_schema = load_schema(\"cad\")\n    logger.info(f\"Schema loaded with {len(cad_schema.get('fields', []))} field definitions\")\nexcept (KeyError, FileNotFoundError) as e:\n    logger.warning(f\"Could not load CAD schema: {e}\")\n    logger.warning(\"Proceeding without schema validation\")\n    cad_schema = {}\n\n# -------------------------------------------------------------------------\n# Step 3: Load source files\n# -------------------------------------------------------------------------\nlogger.info(\"\\n[Step 3/7] Loading source files...\")\n\ndataframes: List[pd.DataFrame] = []\nfile_hashes: Dict[int, str] = {}\n\nfor source in tqdm(sources, desc=\"Loading files\"):\n    df = load_source_file(source)\n    if df is not None:\n        dataframes.append(df)\n        # Compute hash for audit trail\n        filepath = Path(source[\"path\"])\n        if filepath.exists():\n            file_hashes[source[\"year\"]] = compute_file_hash(filepath)\n\nif not dataframes:\n    logger.error(\"No source files loaded successfully\")\n    return None\n\nlogger.info(f\"Successfully loaded {len(dataframes)} files\")\n\n# -------------------------------------------------------------------------\n# Step 4: cad_schema)\n\nlogger.info(\"\\n[Step 6/7] Validating records...\")\n\ndf_validated, validation_results = validate_dataframe(df_normalized, cad_schema)\n\nquality_score = calculate_quality_score(df_validated, validation_results)\nlogger.info(f\"Quality score: {quality_score}/100\")\n\n# -------------------------------------------------------------------------\n# Step {}).get(\"dedup_field\", \"ReportNumberNew\")\ndf_final = deduplicate_records(df_validated, dedup_key)\n\n# Detect gaps\ngap_df = detect_gaps(df_final)\n\n# -------------------------------------------------------------------------\n# Metrics summary\n# -------------------------------------------------------------------------\nend_time = datetime.now()\nduration = (end_time - start_time).total_seconds()\n\nmetrics = {\n    \"run_timestamp\": start_time.isoformat(),\n    \"duration_seconds\": duration,\n    \"source_files\": len(sources),\n    \"files_loaded\": len(dataframes),\n    \"records_combined\": len(df_combined),\n    \"records_final\": len(df_final),\n    \"duplicates_removed\": len(df_combined) - len(df_final),\n    \"quality_score\": quality_score,\n    \"validation_errors\": validation_results.get(\"error_count\", 0),\n    \"gaps_detected\": len(gap_df),\n    \"file_hashes\": file_hashes,\n    \"years_covered\": sorted([s[\"year\"] for s in sources]),\n}\n\nlogger.info(\"\\n\" + \"=\" * 60)\nlogger.info(\"CONSOLIDATION SUMMARY\")\nlogger.info(\"=\" * 60)\nlogger.info(f\"  Source files:      {metrics['files_loaded']}/{metrics['source_files']}\")\nlogger.info(f\"  Records combined:  {metrics['records_combined']:,}\")\nlogger.info(f\"  Duplicates removed:{metrics['duplicates_removed']:,}\")\nlogger.info(f\"  Final records:     {metrics['records_final']:,}\")\nlogger.info(f\"  Quality score:     {metrics['quality_score']}/100\")\nlogger.info(f\"  Gaps detected:     {metrics['gaps_detected']}\")\nlogger.info(f\"  Duration:          {duration:.1f} seconds\")\nlogger.info(\"=\" * 60)\n\nif \"consolidation/output\")\noutput_dir.mkdir(parents=True, exist_ok=True)\n\noutput_file = output_dir / output_config.get(\"consolidated_file\", \"2019_2026_CAD_Consolidated.csv\")\n\nlogger.info(f\"\\nSaving consolidated dataset: {output_file}\")\n\n# Remove internal tracking columns before export\nexport_cols = [c for c in df_final.columns \"FullAddress2\",\n    \"Incident\",\n    \"Officer\",\n    \"BadgeNumber\",\n}\n\n\n=============================================================================\n\n\nNormalizer Functions\n\n\n=============================================================================\n\n\ndef normalize_column_names(df: pd.DataFrame) -> Tuple[pd.DataFrame, Dict[str, str]]:\n    \"\"\"\n    Standardize column names to canonical format.\n\n\nArgs:\n    df: Input DataFrame\n    \nReturns:\n    Tuple of (normalized DataFrame, mapping of old → new names)\n\"\"\"\nrename_map = {}\n\nfor col in df.columns:\n    # Clean the column name\n    clean = col.strip()\n    \n    # Check for direct mapping (case-insensitive)\n    lower = clean.lower().replace(\" \", \"_\").replace(\"-\", \"_\")\n    if lower in COLUMN_NAME_MAPPINGS:\n        rename_map[col] = COLUMN_NAME_MAPPINGS[lower]\n    elif clean != col:\n        # At minimum, strip whitespace\n        rename_map[col] = clean\n\nif rename_map:\n    df = df.rename(columns=rename_map)\n    logger.debug(f\"Renamed {len(rename_map)} columns: {rename_map}\")\n\nreturn df, rename_map\n\n\ndef normalize_how_reported(series: pd.Series) -> pd.Series:\n    \"\"\"\n    Normalize HowReported field using pattern-based domain mapping.\n\n\nArgs:\n    series: Pandas Series containing HowReported values\n    \nReturns:\n    Normalized Series with canonical domain values\n\"\"\"\ndef _normalize_value(val: Any) -> Optional[str]:\n    if pd.isna(val) or val is None:\n        return None\n    \n    # Convert to string and clean\n    s = str(val).strip().upper()\n    \n    if not s:\n        return None\n    \n    # Check direct mapping\n    if s in HOW_REPORTED_MAPPINGS:\n        return HOW_REPORTED_MAPPINGS[s]\n    \n    # Check if already valid (case-insensitive)\n    for valid in HOW_REPORTED_VALID:\n        if s == valid.upper():\n            return valid\n    \n    # Partial matching for common patterns\n    if \"911\" in s or \"9-1-1\" in s:\n        return \"9-1-1\"\n    if \"PHONE\" in s or \"CALL\" in s:\n        return \"Phone\"\n    if \"WALK\" in s:\n        return \"Walk-In\"\n    if \"SELF\" in s or \"OFFICER\" in s:\n        return \"Self-Initiated\"\n    if \"RADIO\" in s:\n        return \"Radio\"\n    if \"ALARM\" in s:\n        return \"Alarm\"\n    if \"WEB\" in s or \"ONLINE\" in s or \"INTERNET\" in s:\n        return \"Online\"\n    if \"REFER\" in s:\n        return \"Referral\"\n    \n    # Default to \"Other\" for unrecognized values\n    logger.debug(f\"HowReported value '{val}' mapped to 'Other'\")\n    return \"Other\"\n\nreturn series.apply(_normalize_value)\n\n\ndef normalize_disposition(series: pd.Series) -> pd.Series:\n    \"\"\"\n    Normalize Disposition field, handling concatenated CamelCase values.\n\n\nArgs:\n    series: Pandas Series containing Disposition values\n    \nReturns:\n    Normalized Series with split/mapped values\n\"\"\"\nconcat_map = CONCATENATED_PATTERNS.get(\"Disposition\", {})\n\ndef _normalize_value(val: Any) -> Optional[str]:\n    if pd.isna(val) or val is None:\n        return None\n    \n    s = str(val).strip()\n    if not s:\n        return None\n    \n    # Check direct mapping for known concatenated values\n    if s in concat_map:\n        return concat_map[s]\n    \n    # Try case-insensitive match\n    s_upper = s.upper()\n    for key, mapped in concat_map.items():\n        if key.upper() == s_upper:\n            return mapped\n    \n    # Split CamelCase if it looks concatenated (no spaces, mixed case)\n    if \" \" not in s and any(c.isupper() for c in s[1:]):\n        # Split on capital letters\n        parts = re.findall(r'[A-Z][a-z]*', s)\n        if len(parts) > 1:\n            # Take first meaningful part (often the main disposition)\n            first_part = parts[0]\n            # Check if first part is in our mapping values\n            for mapped in concat_map.values():\n                if first_part.lower() == mapped.lower():\n                    return mapped\n            return first_part\n    \n    # Return as-is with title case\n    return s.title() if s.islower() or s.isupper() else s\n\nreturn series.apply(_normalize_value)\n\n\ndef normalize_address_usps(series: pd.Series) -> pd.Series:\n    \"\"\"\n    Apply USPS-compliant address formatting.\n\n\nArgs:\n    series: Pandas Series containing address values\n    \nReturns:\n    Normalized Series with USPS standard formatting\n\"\"\"\ndef _normalize_address(val: Any) -> Optional[str]:\n    if pd.isna(val) or val is None:\n        return None\n    \n    s = str(val).strip()\n    if not s:\n        return None\n    \n    # Convert to uppercase for processing\n    addr = s.upper()\n    \n    # Replace street suffixes with abbreviations\n    for full, abbrev in USPS_STREET_SUFFIXES.items():\n        # Match whole word only\n        pattern = rf'\\b{full}\\b\\.? '\n        addr = re.sub(pattern, abbrev, addr, flags=re.IGNORECASE)\n    \n    # Replace directionals with abbreviations\n    for full, abbrev in USPS_DIRECTIONALS.items():\n        pattern = rf'\\b{full}\\b\\.? '\n        addr = re.sub(pattern, abbrev, addr, flags=re.IGNORECASE)\n    \n    # Remove extra whitespace\n    addr = re.sub(r'\\s+', ' ', addr).strip()\n    \n    # Remove trailing periods\n    addr = addr.rstrip('. ')\n    \n    # Standardize apartment/unit notation\n    addr = re.sub(r'\\bAPT\\. ?\\s*#?\\s*', 'APT ', addr)\n    addr = re.sub(r'\\bUNIT\\. ?\\s*#?\\s*', 'UNIT ', addr)\n    addr = re.sub(r'\\bSTE\\. ?\\s*#?\\s*', 'STE ', addr)\n    addr = re.sub(r'\\bSUITE\\. ?\\s*#?\\s*', 'STE ', addr)\n    addr = re.sub(r'\\bFLOOR\\. ?\\s*#?\\s*', 'FL ', addr)\n    addr = re.sub(r'\\bFL\\. ?\\s*#?\\s*', 'FL ', addr)\n    \n    # Remove duplicate spaces again\n    addr = re.sub(r'\\s+', ' ', addr).strip()\n    \n    return addr\n\nreturn series.apply(_normalize_address)\n\n\ndef normalize_case_number(series: pd.Series) -> pd.Series:\n    \"\"\"\n    Normalize case/report numbers preserving as text.\n\n\nHandles formats like: 25-000001, 25-000001A, 2025-000001\n\nArgs:\n    series: Pandas Series containing case numbers\n    \nReturns:\n    Normalized Series with standardized case number format\n\"\"\"\ndef _normalize_case(val: Any) -> Optional[str]:\n    if pd.isna(val) or val is None:\n        return None\n    \n    s = str(val).strip()\n    if not s:\n        return None\n    \n    # Remove any leading/trailing quotes or whitespace\n    s = s.strip(\"'\\\"` \")\n    \n    # Already in correct format (YY-NNNNNN or YY-NNNNNNA)\n    if re.match(r'^\\d{2}-\\d{6}[A-Z]?$', s):\n        return s.upper()\n    \n    # Handle 4-digit year format (YYYY-NNNNNN)\n    match = re.match(r'^(20)?

(\\d{2})-(\\d{6})([A-Z])?$', s, re.IGNORECASE)\n    if match:\n        year = match.group(2)\n        num = match.group(3)\n        suffix = (match.group(4) or \"\").upper()\n        return f\"{year}-{num}{suffix}\"\n    \n    # Handle no-dash format (YYNNNNN or YYNNNNNNA)\n    match = re.match(r'^(\\d{2})(\\d{6})([A-Z])?$', s, re.IGNORECASE)\n    if match:\n        year = match.group(1)\n        num = match.group(2)\n        suffix = (match.group(3) or \"\").upper()\n        return f\"{year}-{num}{suffix}\"\n    \n    # Return original if no pattern matches\n    return s\n\nreturn series.apply(_normalize_case)\n\n\ndef normalize_datetime_field(series: pd.Series, output_format: str = None) -> pd.Series:\n    \"\"\"\n    Normalize datetime fields handling various input formats.\n\n\nArgs:\n    series: Pandas Series containing datetime values\n    output_format: Optional strftime format string for output\n    \nReturns:\n    Normalized Series (datetime64 or formatted string)\n\"\"\"\n# Common datetime formats to try\nformats_to_try = [\n    \"%Y-%m-%d %H:%M:%S\",\n    \"%Y-%m-%d %H:%M\",\n    \"%Y-%m-%d\",\n    \"%m/%d/%Y %H:%M:%S\",\n    \"%m/%d/%Y %H:%M\",\n    \"%m/%d/%Y\",\n    \"%m-%d-%Y %H:%M:%S\",\n    \"%m-%d-%Y\",\n    \"%d/%m/%Y %H:%M:%S\",\n    \"%d/%m/%Y\",\n    \"%Y%m%d%H%M%S\",\n    \"%Y%m%d\",\n]\n\n# Try pandas built-in parser first\ntry:\n    result = pd.to_datetime(series, errors='coerce', infer_datetime_format=True)\n    \n    # If output format specified, convert to string\n    if output_format and result.notna().any():\n        result = result.dt.strftime(output_format).replace('NaT', None)\n    \n    return result\nexcept Exception as e:\n    logger.warning(f\"Datetime normalization failed: {e}\")\n    return series\n\n\ndef normalize_whitespace(series: pd.Series) -> pd.Series:\n    \"\"\"\n    Normalize whitespace in text fields.\n\n\nArgs:\n    series: Pandas Series\n    \nReturns:\n    Series with normalized whitespace\n\"\"\"\ndef _clean(val: Any) -> Optional[str]:\n    if pd.isna(val) or val is None:\n        return None\n    s = str(val)\n    # Replace multiple spaces with single space\n    s = re.sub(r'\\s+', ' ', s)\n    # Strip leading/trailing\n    s = s.strip()\n    return s if s else None\n\nreturn series.apply(_clean)\n\n\ndef coerce_to_string(series: pd.Series)       config_path: Path to validation_rules.yaml\n    \"\"\"\n    try:\n        import yaml\n        \n        with open(config_path, 'r', encoding='utf-8') as f:\n            config = domain_config.items():\n            if 'normalize_patterns' in field_config:\n                # Create mapping from config\n                mapping = field_config['normalize_patterns']\n                valid_values = set(field_config.get('valid_values', []))\n                \n                # Check if we already have a rule for this field\n                existing = [r for r in self.rules if r.field == field_name]\n                if not existing:\n                    rule = NormalizationRule(\n                        field=field_name,\n                        rule_type=NormalizationType.DOMAIN_MAP,\n                        params={\n                            \"mapping\": mapping,\n                            \"valid_values\": valid_values,\n                        },\n                        priority=35,\n                        preserve_original=True,\n                        description=f\"Domain normalization for {field_name} (from config)\",\n                    )\n                    self.rules.append(rule)\n        \n        logger.info(f\"Loaded additional rules from {config_path}\")\n        \n    except Exception as e:\n        logger.warning(f\"Could not load rules from config: {e}\")\n\ndef add_rule(self, rule: NormalizationRule) -> None:\n    \"\"\"\n    Add a normalization rule.\n    \n    Args:\n        rule: None,\n    inplace: bool = False,\n) -> pd.DataFrame:\n    \"\"\"\n    Apply normalization rules to DataFrame.\n    \n    Args:\n        df: Input DataFrame\n        fields: Specific fields to normalize (None = all applicable)\n        inplace: Whether to modify DataFrame in place\n        \n    Returns:\n        Normalized DataFrame\n    \"\"\"\n    if not inplace:\n        df = df.copy()\n    \n    self._results.clear()\n    start_cols = set(df.columns)\n    \n    logger.info(f\"Starting normalization: {len(df):,} records, {len(df.columns)} columns\")\n    \n    # Step 1: Standardize column names\n    df, renamed = normalize_column_names(df)\n    if renamed:\n        logger.info(f\"Renamed {len(renamed)} columns to canonical names\")\n    \n    # Step 2: Apply field-specific rules\n    for rule in self.rules:\n        # Check if field exists or is wildcard\n        if rule.field == \"*\":\n            # Wildcard rules apply to all string columns\n            applicable_cols = df.select_dtypes(include=['object']).columns.tolist()\n        elif rule.field in df.columns:\n            applicable_cols = [rule.field]\n        else:\n            # Try case-insensitive match\n            matched = [c for c in df.columns if c.lower() == rule.field.lower()]\n            if matched:\n                applicable_cols = matched\n            else:\n                continue\n        \n        # Filter to requested fields if specified\n        if fields:\n            applicable_cols = [c for c in applicable_cols if c in fields]\n        \n        if not applicable_cols:\n            continue\n        \n        # Apply rule to each applicable column\n        for col in applicable_cols:\n            self._apply_rule(df, col, rule)\n    \n    # Log summary\n    new_cols = set(df.columns) - start_cols\n    if new_cols:\n        logger.info(f\"Created {len(new_cols)} backup columns: {sorted(new_cols)}\")\n    \n    logger.info(f\"Normalization complete: {len(self._results)} fields processed\")\n    \n    return df\n\ndef _apply_rule(\n    self,\n    df: pd.DataFrame,\n    column: str,\n    rule: NormalizationRule,\n) -> None:\n    \"\"\"\n    Apply a single normalization rule to a column.\n    \n    Args:\n        df: DataFrame to modify\n        column: Column name\n        rule: NormalizationRule to apply\n    \"\"\"\n    if column not in df.columns:\n        return\n    \n    series = df[column]\n    \n    # Track metrics\n    null_before = series.isna().sum()\n    unique_before = series.nunique()\n    \n    # Preserve original if requested\n    if rule.preserve_original or self.preserve_originals:\n        raw_col = f\"_raw_{column}\"\n        if raw_col not in df.columns:\n            df[raw_col] = series.copy()\n    \n    # Get normalizer function\n    normalizer = rule.params.get(\"normalizer\")\n    \n    try:\n        if normalizer and callable(normalizer):\n            # Use provided normalizer function\n            normalized = normalizer(series)\n        elif rule.rule_type == NormalizationType.STRIP_WHITESPACE:\n            normalized = normalize_whitespace(series)\n        elif rule.rule_type == NormalizationType.DOMAIN_MAP:\n            normalized = self._apply_domain_map(series, rule.params)\n        elif rule.rule_type == NormalizationType.CONCATENATED_SPLIT:\n            normalized = self._apply_concat_split(series, rule.params)\n        elif rule.rule_type == NormalizationType.PRESERVE_TEXT:\n            normalized = coerce_to_string(series)\n        elif rule.rule_type == NormalizationType.ADDRESS_FORMAT:\n            normalized = normalize_address_usps(series)\n        else:\n            normalized = series\n        \n        # Update column\n        df[column] = normalized\n        \n        # Track results\n        null_after = df[column].isna().sum()\n        unique_after = df[column].nunique()\n        modified = (series != df[column]).sum()\n        \n        # Sample changes for logging\n        changes = series[series != df[column]]\n        sample_changes = []\n        if len(changes) > 0:\n            sample_idx = changes.head(3).index\n            for idx in sample_idx:\n                sample_changes.append((series.loc[idx], df.loc[idx, column]))\n        \n        self._results[column] = NormalizationResult(\n            field=column,\n            records_processed=len(series),\n            records_modified=modified,\n            null_before=null_before,\n            null_after=null_after,\n            unique_before=unique_before,\n            unique_after=unique_after,\n            sample_changes=sample_changes,\n        )\n        \n        if modified > 0:\n            logger.debug(\n                f\"  {column}: {modified:,} values sample_changes[:2]:\n                    logger.debug(f\"    Example: '{old}' → '{new}'\")\n                    \n    except Exception as e:\n        logger.error(f\"Error normalizing {column}: {e}\")\n        self._results[column] = NormalizationResult(\n            field=column,\n            records_processed=len(series),\n            records_modified=0,\n            null_before=null_before,\n            null_after=null_before,\n            unique_before=unique_before,\n            unique_after=unique_before,\n            errors=[str(e)],\n        )\n\ndef _apply_domain_map(self, series: pd.Series, params: Dict) -> pd.Series:\n    \"\"\"Apply domain mapping normalization.\"\"\"\n    mapping = params.get(\"mapping\", {})\n    valid_values = params.get(\"valid_values\", set())\n    default = params.get(\"default\")\n    \n    def _map_value(val: Any) -> Optional[str]:\n        if pd.isna(val) or val is None:\n            return default if default else None\n        \n        s = str(val).strip()\n        if not s:\n            return default if default else None\n        \n        # Direct mapping lookup (case-insensitive)\n        s_upper = s.upper()\n        if s_upper in mapping:\n            return mapping[s_upper]\n        if s in mapping:\n            return mapping[s]\n        \n        # Check if already valid\n        if valid_values:\n            for valid in valid_values:\n                if s.upper() == valid.upper():\n                    return valid\n        \n        # Return default or original\n        return default if default else s\n    \n    return series.apply(_map_value)\n\ndef _apply_concat_split(self, series: pd.Series, params: Dict) -> pd.Series:\n    \"\"\"Apply concatenated value splitting.\"\"\"\n    mapping = params.get(\"mapping\", {})\n    \n    def _split_value(val: Any) -> Optional[str]:\n        if pd.isna(val) or val is None:\n            return None\n        \n        s = str(val).strip()\n        if not s:\n            return None\n        \n        # Direct mapping lookup\n        if s in mapping:\n            return mapping[s]\n        \n        # Case-insensitive lookup\n        for key, mapped in mapping.items():\n            if key.upper() == s.upper():\n                return mapped\n        \n        # CamelCase split\n        if \" \" not in s and re.search(r'[a-z][A-Z]', s):\n            parts = re.findall(r'[A-Z][a-z]*', s)\n            if parts:\n                return parts[0]\n        \n        return s\n    \n    return series.apply(_split_value)\n\ndef get_results(self) -> Dict[str, NormalizationResult]:\n    \"\"\"Get normalization results for all processed fields.\"\"\"\n    return self._results.copy()\n\ndef get_summary(self) -> str:\n    \"\"\"Generate human-readable normalization summary.\"\"\"\n    lines = [\n        \"Normalization Summary\",\n        \"=\" * 50,\n    ]\n    \n    total_modified = 0\n    for field, result in sorted(self._results.items()):\n        total_modified += result.records_modified\n        if result.records_modified > 0 or result.errors:\n            status = \"⚠️\" if      )\n            if result.errors:\n                for err in result.errors:\n                    lines.append(f\"    ERROR: {err}\")\n    \n    lines.append(\"=\" * 50)\n    lines.append(f\"Total results for a single field.\"\"\"\n    field: str\n    total_records: int\n    valid_count: int\n    invalid_count: int\n    null_count: int\n    error_count: int = 0\n    warning_count: int = 0\n    validation_rate: float = 0.0\n    rules_applied: List[str] = field(default_factory=list)\n    sample_errors: List[Dict[str, Any]] = field(default_factory=list)\n\n\ndef __post_init__(self):\n    if self.total_records > 0:\n        non_null = self.total_records - self.null_count\n        if non_null > 0:\n            self.validation_rate = round(self.valid_count / non_null * 100, 2)\n\n\n@dataclass\nclass ValidationResult:\n    \"\"\"Complete validation results for a DataFrame.\"\"\"\n    total_records: int\n    valid_records: int\n    invalid_records: int\n    error_count: int\n    warning_count: int\n    fields_validated: int\n    rules_applied: int\n    validation_rate: float\n    duration_seconds: float\n    timestamp: str\n    field_results: Dict[str, FieldValidationResult] = field(default_factory=dict)\n    errors: List[Dict[str, Any]] = field(default_factory=list)\n    warnings: List[Dict[str, Any]] = field(default_factory=list)\n\n\ndef to_dict(self) -> Dict[str, Any]:\n    \"\"\"Convert to dictionary for JSON serialization.\"\"\"\n    return {\n        \"summary\": {\n            \"total_records\": self.total_records,\n            \"valid_records\": self.valid_records,\n            \"invalid_records\": self.invalid_records,\n            \"error_count\": self.error_count,\n            \"warning_count\": self.warning_count,\n            \"fields_validated\": self.fields_validated,\n            \"rules_applied\": self.rules_applied,\n            \"validation_rate\": self.validation_rate,\n            \"duration_seconds\": self.duration_seconds,\n            \"timestamp\": self.timestamp,\n        },\n        \"field_results\": {\n            k: {\n                \"total_records\": v.total_records,\n \"warning_count\": v.warning_count,\n                \"validation_rate\": v.validation_rate,\n                \"rules_applied\": v.rules_applied,\n                \"sample_errors\": v.sample_errors[:5],  # Limit samples\n            }\n            for k, v in self.field_results.items()\n        },\n        \"errors\": self.errors[:100],  # Limit error list\n        \"warnings\": self.warnings[:100],\n    }\n\n\n=============================================================================\n\n\nDefault Validation Rules for CAD Data\n\n\n=============================================================================\n\n\nCase number pattern: YY-NNNNNN or YY-NNNNNNA\n\n\nCASE_NUMBER_PATTERN = r'^\\d{2}-\\d{6}[A-Z]?$'\n\n\nValid \"Transfer\"\n}\n\n\nValid disposition patterns (partial list - actual would come from schema)\n\n\nDISPOSITION_DOMAIN: Set[str] = {\n    \"Arrested\", \"Cleared\", \"Dispersed\", \"GOA\", \"No Action Required\",\n    \"Report\", \"Referred\", \"Unfounded\", \"Warning\", \"Citation\", \n    \"Summons\", \"Transported\", \"Cancelled\", \"Assisted\", \"Advised\",\n    \"Unable to Locate\", \"Civil Matter\", \"Completed\",\n}\n\n\nPDZone patterns (typically A1, A2, B1, etc. )\n\n\nPDZONE_PATTERN = r'^[A-Z]\\d$'\n\n\nTime pattern (HH:MM:SS or HH:MM)\n\n\nTIME_PATTERN = r'^\\d{1,2}:\\d{2}(:\\d{2})?

(\\s*[AP]M)?$'\n\n\nDate patterns\n\n\nDATE_PATTERNS = [\n    r'^\\d{4}-\\d{2}-\\d{2}$',           # ISO: 2025-01-30\n    r'^\\d{2}/\\d{2}/\\d{4}$',           # US: 01/30/2025\n    r'^\\d{1,2}/\\d{1,2}/\\d{4}$',       # US flexible\n]\n\n\ndef build_default_cad_rules() -> List[ValidationRule]:\n    \"\"\"\n    Build default validation rules for CAD data based on Functions\n\n\n=============================================================================\n\n\ndef validate_required_vectorized(series: pd.Series) -> pd.Series:\n    \"\"\"\n    Vectorized required field validation.\n\n\nArgs:\n    series: Pandas Series to validate\n    \nReturns:\n    Boolean Series (True = valid, False = invalid)\n\"\"\"\n# Check for null, empty string, or whitespace-only\nis_valid = series.notna()\n\n# For string columns, also check for empty/whitespace\nif series.dtype == 'object':\n    is_valid = is_valid & (series.astype(str).str.strip() != '')\n    is_valid = is_valid & (series.astype(str).str.lower() != 'nan')\n    is_valid = is_valid & (series.astype(str).str.lower() != 'none')\n\nreturn is_valid\n\n\ndef validate_regex_vectorized(series: pd.Series, pattern: str, allow_null: bool = False) -> pd.Series:\n    \"\"\"\n    Vectorized regex pattern validation.\n\n\nArgs:\n    series: Pandas Series to validate\n    pattern: Regex pattern to match\n    allow_null: Whether null values are considered valid\n    \nReturns:\n    Boolean Series (True = valid, False = invalid)\n\"\"\"\n# Handle nulls\nis_null = series.isna()\n\nif allow_null:\n    # Nulls are valid, check pattern only on non-nulls\n    is_valid = is_null.copy()\n    non_null_mask = ~is_null\n    if non_null_mask.any():\n        is_valid[non_null_mask] = series[non_null_mask].astype(str).str.match(pattern, na=False)\nelse:\n    # Nulls are invalid\n    is_valid = series.astype(str).str.match(pattern, na=False)\n\nreturn is_valid\n\n\ndef validate_domain_vectorized(\n    series: pd.Series,\n    valid_values: Set[str],\n    case_sensitive: bool = False,\n    allow_null: bool = True,\n    partial_match: bool = False,\n) -> pd.Series:\n    \"\"\"\n    Vectorized domain/controlled vocabulary validation.\n\n\nArgs:\n    series: Pandas Series to validate\n    valid_values: Set of allowed values\n    case_sensitive: Whether comparison is case-sensitive\n    allow_null: Whether null values are considered valid\n    partial_match: Allow partial string matches\n    \nReturns:\n    Boolean Series (True = valid, False = invalid)\n\"\"\"\nis_null = series.isna()\n\nif not case_sensitive:\n    valid_upper = {v.upper() for v in valid_values}\n    check_series = series.astype(str).str.upper().str.strip()\nelse:\n    valid_upper = valid_values\n    check_series = series.astype(str).str.strip()\n\nif partial_match:\n    # Check if any valid value is contained in the field\n    def _partial_check(val):\n        if pd.isna(val):\n            return allow_null\n        val_str = str(val).upper() if not case_sensitive else str(val)\n        return any(v in val_str or val_str in v for v in valid_upper)\n    \n    is_valid = series.apply(_partial_check)\nelse:\n    is_valid = check_series.isin(valid_upper)\n\n# Handle nulls\nif allow_null:\n    is_valid = is_valid | is_null\n\nreturn is_valid\n\n\ndef validate_range_vectorized(\n    series: pd.Series,\n    min_val: Optional[float] = None,\n    max_val: Optional[float] = None,\n    allow_null: bool = True,\n) -> pd.Series:\n    \"\"\"\n    Vectorized numeric range validation.\n\n\nArgs:\n    series: Pandas Series to validate\n    min_val: Minimum allowed value (inclusive)\n    max_val: Maximum allowed value (inclusive)\n    allow_null: Whether null values are considered valid\n    \nReturns:\n    Boolean Series (True = valid, False = invalid)\n\"\"\"\n# Convert to numeric\nnumeric = pd.to_numeric(series, errors='coerce')\nis_null = numeric.isna()\n\nis_valid = pd.Series([True] * len(series), index=series.index)\n\nif min_val is not None:\n    is_valid = is_valid & (numeric >= min_val)\nif max_val is not None:\n    is_valid = is_valid & (numeric <= max_val)\n\n# Handle nulls\nif allow_null:\n    is_valid = is_valid | is_null\nelse:\n    is_valid = is_valid & ~is_null\n\nreturn is_valid\n\n\ndef validate_length_vectorized(\n    series: pd.Series,\n    min_length: Optional[int] = None,\n    max_length: Optional[int] = None,\n    allow_null: bool = True,\n) -> pd.Series:\n    \"\"\"\n    Vectorized string length validation.\n\n\nArgs:\n    series: Pandas Series to validate\n    min_length: Minimum string length\n    max_length: Maximum string length\n    allow_null: Whether null values are considered valid\n    \nReturns:\n    Boolean Series (True = valid, False = invalid)\n\"\"\"\nis_null = series.isna()\nlengths = series.astype(str).str.len()\n\nis_valid = pd.Series([True] * len(series), index=series.index)\n\nif min_length is not None:\n    is_valid = is_valid & (lengths >= min_length)\nif max_length is not None:\n    is_valid = is_valid & (lengths <= max_length)\n\n# Handle nulls\nif allow_null:\n    is_valid = is_valid | is_null\nelse:\n    is_valid = is_valid & ~is_null\n\nreturn is_valid\n\n\ndef validate_unique_vectorized(series: pd.Series) -> Tuple[pd.Series, int]:\n    \"\"\"\n    Vectorized uniqueness validation.\n\n\nArgs:\n    series: Pandas Series to validate\n    \nReturns:\n    Tuple of (Boolean Series marking duplicates, duplicate count)\n\"\"\"\n# Mark all occurrences of duplicates (not just subsequent ones)\nduplicated = series.duplicated(keep=False)\n\n# First occurrence is valid, subsequent are invalid\nis_valid = ~series.duplicated(keep='first')\n\n# Null values don't count as duplicates\nis_null = series.isna()\nis_valid = is_valid | is_null\n\ndup_count = duplicated.sum() - series.duplicated(keep='first').sum()\n\nreturn is_valid, dup_count\n\n\ndef validate_date_format_vectorized(\n    series: pd.Series,\n    formats: Optional[List[str]] = None,\n    allow_null: bool = True,\n) -> pd.Series:\n    \"\"\"\n    Vectorized date format validation.\n\n\nArgs:\n    series: Pandas Series to validate\n    formats: List of acceptable date formats\n    allow_null: Whether null values are considered valid\n    \nReturns:\n    Boolean Series (True = valid, False = invalid)\n\"\"\"\nif formats is None:\n    formats = DATE_PATTERNS\n\nis_null = series.isna()\n\n# Try parsing with pandas\ntry:\n    parsed = pd.to_datetime(series, errors='coerce', infer_datetime_format=True)\n    is_valid = parsed.notna()\nexcept Exception:\n    # Fall back to regex matching\n    is_valid = pd.Series([False] * len(series), index=series.index)\n    str_series = series.astype(str)\n    for pattern in formats:\n        is_valid = is_valid | str_series.str.match(pattern, na=False)\n\n# Handle nulls\nif allow_null:\n    is_valid = is_valid | is_null\n\nreturn is_valid\n\n\n=============================================================================\n\n\nValidation Engine Class\n\n\n=============================================================================\n\n\nclass ValidationEngine:\n    \"\"\"\n    Schema-driven validation engine with parallel processing support.\n\n\nProvides comprehensive data validation with:\n- Required field checking\n- Regex pattern compliance\n- Domain/vocabulary enforcement\n- Range and length validation\n- Uniqueness checks\n- Parallel/vectorized processing\n\nAttributes:\n    rules: List of ValidationRule objects\n    schema: Optional JSON schema for field definitions\n    parallel: Whether to use parallel processing\n    max_workers: Number of parallel workers\n\"\"\"\n\ndef __init__(\n    self,\n    rules: Optional[List[ValidationRule]] = None,\n    schema: Optional[Dict] = None,\n    config_path: Optional[Path] = None,\n    parallel: bool = True,\n    max_workers: Optional[int] = None,\n):\n    \"\"\"\n    Initialize ValidationEngine.\n    \n    Args:\n        rules: Custom validation rules (uses CAD defaults if None)\n        schema: JSON schema with field definitions\n        config_path: Path to validation_rules.yaml for additional rules\n        parallel: Enable parallel processing for large datasets\n        max_workers: Number of parallel workers (None = auto)\n    \"\"\"\n    self.schema = schema or {}\n    self.parallel = parallel\n    self.max_workers = max_workers\n    self.rules = rules or build_default_cad_rules()\n    self._results: Optional[ValidationResult] = None\n    \n    # Load additional rules from config\n    if config_path:\n        self._load_rules_from_config(config_path)\n    \n    # Build rules from schema if provided\n    if schema:\n        self._build_rules_from_schema(schema)\n    \n    logger.debug(f\"ValidationEngine initialized with {len(self.rules)} rules\")\n\ndef _load_rules_from_config(self, config_path: Path) -> None:\n    \"\"\"\n    Load additional validation rules from validation_rules.yaml.\n    \n    Args:\n        config_path: Path to validation_rules.yaml\n    \"\"\"\n    try:\n        import yaml\n        \n        with open(config_path, 'r', encoding='utf-8') as f:\n            config = yaml.safe_load(f)\n        \n        # Load required fields\n        required_fields = config.get('required_fields', {})\n        for source_type, fields in required_fields.items():\n            for field_name in fields:\n                # Check if rule already exists\n                exists = any(\n                    r.field == field_name and r.rule_type == ValidationType.REQUIRED\n                    for r in self.rules\n                )\n                if not exists:\n                    self.rules.append(ValidationRule(\n                        field=field_name,\n                        rule_type=ValidationType.REQUIRED,\n                        severity=ValidationSeverity.ERROR,\n                        message=f\"{field_name} is required\",\n                        description=f\"Required field from config ({source_type})\",\n                    ))\n        \n        # Load case number pattern\n        case_config = config.get('case_number', {})\n        if 'pattern' in case_config:\n            # Update existing rule or add new\n            for rule in self.rules:\n                if rule.field == 'ReportNumberNew' and rule.rule_type == ValidationType.REGEX:\n                    rule.params['pattern'] = case_config['pattern']\n                    break\n        \n        # Load domain validation\n        domain_config = config.get('domain_validation', {})\n        for field_name, field_config in domain_config.items():\n            valid_values = set(field_config.get('valid_values', []))\n            if valid_values:\n                # Check for existing domain rule\n                exists = any(\n                    r.field == field_name and r.rule_type == ValidationType.DOMAIN\n                    for r in self.rules\n                )\n                if not exists:\n                    self.rules.append(ValidationRule(\n                        field=field_name,\n                        rule_type=ValidationType.DOMAIN,\n                        params={\n                            \"values\": valid_values,\n                            \"case_sensitive\": False,\n                        },\n                        severity=ValidationSeverity.WARNING,\n                        message=f\"{field_name} value not in valid domain\",\n                        description=f\"Domain validation from config\",\n                    ))\n        \n        logger.info(f\"Loaded validation rules from {config_path}\")\n        \n    except Exception as e:\n        logger.warning(f\"Could not load rules from config: {e}\")\n\ndef _build_rules_from_schema(self, schema: Dict) -> None:\n    \"\"\"\n    Build validation rules from JSON schema.\n    \n    Args:\n        schema: JSON schema with field definitions\n    \"\"\"\n    fields = schema.get('fields', schema.get('properties', {}))\n    \n    for field_name, field_def in fields.items():\n        if isinstance(field_def, dict):\n            # Required check\n            if field_def.get('required', False):\n                exists = any(\n                    r.field == field_name and r.rule_type == ValidationType.REQUIRED\n                    for r in self.rules\n                )\n                if not exists:\n                    self.rules.append(ValidationRule(\n                        field=field_name,\n                        rule_type=ValidationType.REQUIRED,\n                        severity=ValidationSeverity.ERROR,\n                        message=f\"{field_name} is required (from schema)\",\n                    ))\n            \n            # Pattern check\n            if 'pattern' in field_def:\n                exists = any(\n                    r.field == field_name and r.rule_type == ValidationType.REGEX\n                    for r in self.rules\n                )\n                if not exists:\n                    self.rules.append(ValidationRule(\n                        field=field_name,\n                        rule_type=ValidationType.REGEX,\n                        params={\"pattern\": field_def['pattern']},\n                        severity=ValidationSeverity.WARNING,\n                        message=f\"{field_name} format invalid\",\n                    ))\n            \n            # Enum/domain check\n            if 'enum' in field_def:\n                exists = any(\n                    r.field == field_name and r.rule_type == ValidationType.DOMAIN\n                    for r in self.rules\n                )\n                if not exists:\n                    self.rules.append(ValidationRule(\n                        field=field_name,\n                        rule_type=ValidationType.DOMAIN,\n                        params={\"values\": set(field_def['enum'])},\n                        severity=ValidationSeverity.WARNING,\n                        message=f\"{field_name} value not in allowed list\",\n                    ))\n            \n            # Length constraints\n            min_len = field_def.get('minLength')\n            max_len = field_def.get('maxLength')\n            if min_len is not None or max_len is not None:\n                self.rules.append(ValidationRule(\n                    field=field_name,\n                    rule_type=ValidationType.LENGTH,\n                    params={\"min_length\": min_len, \"max_length\": max_len},\n                    severity=ValidationSeverity.WARNING,\n                    message=f\"{field_name} length out of range\",\n                ))\n\ndef add_rule(self, rule: ValidationRule) -> None:\n    \"\"\"\n    Add a validation rule.\n    \n    Args:\n        rule: ValidationRule to add\n    \"\"\"\n    self.rules.append(rule)\n\ndef validate(\n    self,\n    df: pd.DataFrame,\n    schema: Optional[Dict] = None,\n    fields: Optional[List[str]] = None,\n) -> ValidationResult:\n    \"\"\"\n    Validate DataFrame against rules and schema.\n    \n    Args:\n        df: DataFrame to validate\n        schema: Optional schema override\n        fields: Specific fields to validate (None = all)\n        \n    Returns:\n        ValidationResult with comprehensive metrics\n    \"\"\"\n    start_time = datetime.now()\n    \n    if schema:\n        self.schema = schema\n        self._build_rules_from_schema(schema)\n    \n    total_records = len(df)\n    logger.info(f\"Starting validation: {total_records:,} records, {len(self.rules)} rules\")\n    \n    # Initialize tracking\n    field_results: Dict[str, FieldValidationResult] = {}\n    all_errors: List[Dict[str, Any]] = []\n    all_warnings: List[Dict[str, Any]] = []\n    record_validity = pd.Series([True] * total_records, index=df.index)\n    rules_applied = 0\n    \n    # Group rules by field for efficient processing\n    field_rules: Dict[str, List[ValidationRule]] = {}\n    for rule in self.rules:\n        if not rule.enabled:\n            continue\n        if rule.field not in field_rules:\n            field_rules[rule.field] = []\n        field_rules[rule.field].append(rule)\n    \n    # Process each field\n    for field_name, rules in field_rules.items():\n        # Skip if field not in DataFrame\n        if field_name not in df.columns:\n            # Check if any required rules\n            for rule in rules:\n                if rule.rule_type == ValidationType.REQUIRED:\n                    all_errors.append({\n                        \"field\": field_name,\n                        \"rule\": \"required\",\n                        \"message\": f\"Required field '{field_name}' not found in data\",\n                        \"severity\": \"error\",\n                    })\n            continue\n        \n        # Skip if not in requested fields\n        if fields and field_name not in fields:\n            continue\n        \n        # Validate this field\n        result = self._validate_field(df, field_name, rules)\n        field_results[field_name] = result\n        rules_applied += len(result.rules_applied)\n        \n        # Update record validity\n        if result.invalid_count > 0:\n            # Get invalid mask from sample errors\n            for err in result.sample_errors:\n                if 'index' in err:\n                    record_validity.loc[err['index']] = False\n        \n        # Collect errors and warnings\n        for err in result.sample_errors:\n            if err.get('severity') == 'error':\n                all_errors.append(err)\n            else:\n                all_warnings.append(err)\n    \n    # Calculate summary metrics\n    end_time = datetime.now()\n    duration = (end_time - start_time).total_seconds()\n    \n    valid_records = record_validity.sum()\n    invalid_records = total_records - valid_records\n    validation_rate = round(valid_records / total_records * 100, 2) if total_records > 0 else 0\n    \n    self._results = ValidationResult(\n        total_records=total_records,\n        valid_records=int(valid_records),\n        invalid_records=int(invalid_records),\n        error_count=len(all_errors),\n        warning_count=len(all_warnings),\n        fields_validated=len(field_results),\n        rules_applied=rules_applied,\n        validation_rate=validation_rate,\n        duration_seconds=duration,\n        timestamp=start_time.isoformat(),\n        field_results=field_results,\n        errors=all_errors,\n        warnings=all_warnings,\n    )\n    \n    logger.info(\n        f\"Validation complete: {valid_records:,}/{total_records:,} valid \"\n        f\"({validation_rate}%), {len(all_errors)} errors, {len(all_warnings)} warnings\"\n    )\n    \n    return self._results\n\ndef _validate_field(\n    self,\n    df: pd.DataFrame,\n    field_name: str,\n    rules: List[ValidationRule],\n) -> FieldValidationResult:\n    \"\"\"\n    Validate a single field against its rules.\n    \n    Args:\n        df: DataFrame containing the field\n        field_name: Name of field to validate\n        rules: List of rules to apply\n        \n    Returns:\n        FieldValidationResult with metrics\n    \"\"\"\n    series = df[field_name]\n    total = len(series)\n    null_count = int(series.isna().sum())\n    \n    # Track validity across all rules\n    combined_validity = pd.Series([True] * total, index=df.index)\n    rules_applied = []\n    sample_errors = []\n    error_count = 0\n    warning_count = 0\n    \n    for rule in rules:\n        if not rule.enabled:\n            continue\n        \n        rules_applied.append(f\"{rule.rule_type.value}:{rule.field}\")\n        \n        # Apply appropriate validation\n        try:\n            validity = self._apply_rule(series, rule)\n            \n            # Combine with overall validity (AND logic)\n            combined_validity = combined_validity & validity\n            \n            # Collect sample errors\n            invalid_mask = ~validity & series.notna()\n            invalid_count = int(invalid_mask.sum())\n            \n            if invalid_count > 0:\n                if rule.severity == ValidationSeverity.ERROR:\n                    error_count += invalid_count\n                else:\n                    warning_count += invalid_count\n                \n                # Sample some errors for reporting\n                sample_indices = invalid_mask[invalid_mask].head(5).index\n                for idx in sample_indices:\n                    sample_errors.append({\n                        \"field\": field_name,\n                        \"rule\": rule.rule_type.value,\n                        \"index\": idx,\n                        \"value\": str(series.loc[idx])[:100],  # Truncate long values\n                        \"message\": rule.message or f\"Validation failed: {rule.rule_type.value}\",\n                        \"severity\": rule.severity.value,\n                    })\n                    \n        except Exception as e:\n            logger.warning(f\"Rule {rule.rule_type.value} failed on {field_name}: {e}\")\n            sample_errors.append({\n                \"field\": field_name,\n                \"rule\": rule.rule_type.value,\n                \"message\": f\"Rule execution error: {str(e)}\",\n                \"severity\": \"error\",\n            })\n    \n    valid_count = int(combined_validity.sum())\n    invalid_count = total - valid_count\n    \n    return FieldValidationResult(\n        field=field_name,\n        total_records=total,\n        valid_count=valid_count,\n        invalid_count=invalid_count,\n        null_count=null_count,\n        error_count=error_count,\n        warning_count=warning_count,\n        rules_applied=rules_applied,\n        sample_errors=sample_errors,\n    )\n\ndef _apply_rule(self, series: pd.Series, rule: ValidationRule) -> pd.Series:\n    \"\"\"\n    Apply a single validation rule to a series.\n    \n    Args:\n        series: Pandas Series to validate\n        rule: ValidationRule to apply\n        \n    Returns:\n        Boolean Series (True = valid)\n    \"\"\"\n    params = rule.params\n    \n    if rule.rule_type == ValidationType.REQUIRED:\n        return validate_required_vectorized(series)\n    \n    elif rule.rule_type == ValidationType.REGEX:\n        pattern = params.get('pattern', '.

*')\n        allow_null = params.get('allow_null', True)\n        return validate_regex_vectorized(series, pattern, allow_null)\n    \n    elif rule.rule_type == ValidationType.DOMAIN:\n        values = params.get('values', set())\n        case_sensitive = params.get('case_sensitive', False)\n        allow_null = params.get('allow_null', True)\n        partial_match = params.get('partial_match', False)\n        return validate_domain_vectorized(\n            series, values, case_sensitive, allow_null, partial_match\n        )\n    \n    elif rule.rule_type == ValidationType.RANGE:\n        min_val = params.get('min')\n        max_val = params.get('max')\n        allow_null = params.get('allow_null', True)\n        return validate_range_vectorized(series, min_val, max_val, allow_null)\n    \n    elif rule.rule_type == ValidationType.LENGTH:\n        min_len = params.get('min_length')\n        max_len = params.get('max_length')\n        allow_null = params.get('allow_null', True)\n        return validate_length_vectorized(series, min_len, max_len, allow_null)\n    \n    elif rule.rule_type == ValidationType.UNIQUE:\n        validity, _ = validate_unique_vectorized(series)\n        return validity\n    \n    elif rule.rule_type == ValidationType.DATE_FORMAT:\n        formats = params.get('formats')\n        allow_null = params.get('allow_null', True)\n        return validate_date_format_vectorized(series, formats, allow_null)\n    \n    elif rule.rule_type == ValidationType.CUSTOM:\n        # Custom validation function\n        validator = params.get('validator')\n        if callable(validator):\n            return series.apply(validator)\n        return pd.Series([True] * len(series), index=series.index)\n    \n    else:\n        # Unknown rule type - pass all\n        logger.warning(f\"Unknown validation type: {rule.rule_type}\")\n        return pd.Series([True] * len(series), index=series.index)\n\ndef get_results(self) -> Optional[ValidationResult]:\n    \"\"\"Get the most recent validation results.\"\"\"\n    return self._results\n\ndef get_summary(self) -> str:\n    \"\"\"Generate human-readable validation summary.\"\"\"\n    if not self._results:\n        return \"No validation has been performed yet.\"\n    \n    r = self._results\n    lines = [\n        \"=\" * 60,\n        \"VALIDATION SUMMARY\",\n        \"=\" * 60,\n        f\"Timestamp:        {r.timestamp}\",\n        f\"Duration:         {r.duration_seconds:.2f} seconds\",\n        f\"Total Records:    {r.total_records:,}\",\n \"FIELD RESULTS:\",\n        \"-\" * 60,\n    ]\n    \n    for field, result in sorted(r.field_results.items()):\n        status = \"✓\" if result.invalid_count == 0 else \"✗\"\n lines.append(f\"      - {err.get('message', 'Unknown error')}\")\n    \n    lines.append(\"=\" * 60)\n    \n    return \"\\n\".join(lines)\n\n\n=============================================================================\n\n\nConvenience Functions\n\n\n=============================================================================\n\n\ndef validate_dataframe(\n    df: pd.DataFrame,\n    schema: Optional[Dict] = None,\n    rules:
